	TUR_balkan_war_intervention_decision = {
		allowed = {
			original_tag = TUR
		}
		target_trigger = {
			FROM = {
				tag = BUL
			}
		}
		available = {
			is_subject = no
			BUL = {
				has_war_with = SER
				owns_state = 756
			}
			TUR = {
				is_in_faction = no
			}
			ROM = {
				has_war_with = BUL
			}
		}
		visible = {
			NOT = {
				has_global_flag = kis_secondbalkanwar_victory
			}
			NOT = {
				has_global_flag = kis_secondbalkanwar_lose
			}
			BUL = {
				has_war_with = SER
			}
			NOT = {
				is_in_faction_with = GER
				has_war_together_with = GER
				is_in_faction_with = FRA
				has_war_together_with = FRA
			}
			SER = {
				NOT = {
					is_in_faction_with = GER
					has_war_together_with = GER
					is_in_faction_with = FRA
					has_war_together_with = FRA
				}
			}
			BUL = {
				NOT = {
					is_in_faction_with = GER
					has_war_together_with = GER
					is_in_faction_with = FRA
					has_war_together_with = FRA
				}
			}
		}
		fire_only_once = yes
		days_remove = 10
		war_with_on_remove = BUL
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					ROM = {
						OR = {
							has_capitulated = yes
							surrender_progress > 0.1
						}
					}
					SER = {
						OR = {
							has_capitulated = yes
							surrender_progress > 0.1
						}
					}
					AND = {
						GRE = {
							has_war_with = BUL
							OR = {
								has_capitulated = yes
								surrender_progress > 0.1
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		remove_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = ww1_secondbalkan.9
			}
		}
	}

	TUR_pay_our_debt = {
		icon = gre_investment_decisions
		allowed = {
			tag = TUR
		}
		fire_only_once = yes
		cost = 300
		visible = {
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					has_completed_focus = TUR_stop_debt_repayment
					has_completed_focus = TUR_dissolve_debt_council
				}
			}
			NOT = {
				has_focus_tree = turkey2_focus_tree
			}
		}
		available = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						tag = TRR
					}
				}
				has_completed_focus = TUR_reset_debt_obligations
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = TUR_pay_our_debt_tooltip
				check_variable = {
					var = opda_lira
					value = 0
					compare = less_than_or_equals
				}
			}
		}
		complete_effect = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_well_dissolve_opda
			clear_variable = opda_lira
			clear_variable = opda_consumer_goods
			clear_variable = opda_resources_to_market
			hidden_effect = {
				remove_dynamic_modifier = {
					modifier = TUR_OPDA
				}
			}
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 5
		}
	}

			}
			NOT = {

			}
			NOT = {

					tooltip = TUR_OPDA_trigger_tooltip
					NOT = {

					}
				}

				has_focus_tree = turkey2_focus_tree
			}
		}
		complete_effect = {
			set_country_flag = {
				flag = has_active_purchase_contract
				days = 60
				value = 1
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_completed_focus = TUR_german_ottoman_arms_deal
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_add_debt_0295
				add_to_variable = {
					opda_lira = 0.295
				}
				add_to_variable = {
					opda_consumer_goods = 0.01
				}
				add_to_variable = {
					opda_resources_to_market = 0.005
				}
			}
			else = {
				custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_add_debt_0590
				add_to_variable = {
					opda_lira = 0.590
				}
				add_to_variable = {
					opda_consumer_goods = 0.02
				}
				add_to_variable = {
					opda_resources_to_market = 0.01
				}
			}
			add_to_variable = {
				opda_resources_to_market = 0.01
			}
		}
		remove_effect = {
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
				type = infantry_equipment_0
				amount = 7000
				producer = GER
			}
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 0.1
			modifier = {
				OR = {
					num_of_civilian_factories < 5
					stockpile_ratio = {
						archetype = infantry_equipment
						ratio > 1
					}
				}
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				has_war = yes
				factor = 10
			}
		}

TUR_reclaiming_ahd_i_milli = {
	TUR_border_skirmishes = {
		icon = border_war

		target_array = neighbors

		available = {
			FROM = {
				any_owned_state = {
					is_controlled_by = FROM
					any_neighbor_state = {
						is_fully_controlled_by = ROOT
						set_temp_variable = { var:attacker_state_temp = id }
						has_ROOT_at_least_1_div_in_current_state_scope = yes
						hidden_trigger = { NOT = { has_state_flag = border_incident_active } }
					}
					NOT = { has_state_flag = border_incident_active }
					set_temp_variable = { var:defender_state_temp = id }
				}
			}
			NOT = { has_non_aggression_pact_with = FROM }
		}

		visible = {
            has_completed_focus = TUR_disobey_the_treaties
			FROM = { exists = yes }
			NOT = { has_war_with = FROM }
			FROM = { has_not_initiated_border_incident_with_ROOT = yes }
			FROM = {
				NOT = {
					is_subject_of = ROOT
				}
				NOT = {
					is_in_faction_with = ROOT
				}
			}
			NOT = {
				is_subject_of = FROM
			}

			NOT = { has_border_war_with = FROM }
			FROM = {
				any_owned_state = {
					is_claimed_by = ROOT
					hidden_trigger = { NOT = { has_state_flag = border_incident_active } }
					any_neighbor_state = {
						hidden_trigger = { NOT = { has_state_flag = border_incident_active } }
						is_fully_controlled_by = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			base = 0
		}

		cost = 50

		fire_only_once = no

		days_remove = 7
		days_re_enable = 15

		complete_effect = {
			hidden_effect = {
				FROM = {
					random_owned_controlled_state = {
						limit = {
							is_claimed_by = ROOT
							hidden_trigger = { NOT = { has_state_flag = border_incident_active } }
							any_neighbor_state = {
								hidden_trigger = { NOT = { has_state_flag = border_incident_active } }
								has_ROOT_at_least_1_div_in_current_state_scope = yes
								is_fully_controlled_by = ROOT
							}
						}
						save_event_target_as = defender_state
						set_variable = { FROM.defender_state_vs_@ROOT = id }
						set_temp_variable = { defender_state_temp = id }
						set_state_flag = border_incident_active
					}
				}
				random_state = {
					limit = {
						is_fully_controlled_by = ROOT
						hidden_trigger = { NOT = { has_state_flag = border_incident_active } }
						has_ROOT_at_least_1_div_in_current_state_scope = yes
						any_neighbor_state = {
							state = var:FROM.defender_state_vs_@ROOT
						}
					}
					save_event_target_as = attacker_state
					set_variable = { FROM.attacker_state_vs_@ROOT = id }
					set_temp_variable = { attacker_state_temp = id }
					set_state_flag = border_incident_active
				}
			}
		}
		remove_effect = {
			start_border_war = {
				change_state_after_war = yes
				attacker = {
					state = var:FROM.attacker_state_vs_@ROOT
					num_provinces = 4
					on_win = wtt_border_conflict_won_attacker.1
					on_lose = wtt_border_conflict_lost_attacker.1
					on_cancel = wtt_border_conflict_canceled_attacker.1
				}
				
				defender = {
					state = var:FROM.defender_state_vs_@ROOT
					num_provinces = 4
					on_win = wtt_border_conflict_won_defender.1
					on_lose = wtt_border_conflict_lost_defender.1
					on_cancel = wtt_border_conflict_canceled_defender.1
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { is_border_conflict_defender_vs_FROM = yes }
				var:attacker_state_vs_@FROM = {
					clr_state_flag = border_incident_active
				}
				var:defender_state_vs_@FROM = {
					clr_state_flag = border_incident_active
				}
				clear_variable = attacker_state_vs_@FROM
				clear_variable = defender_state_vs_@FROM
			}
			else = {
				FROM = {
					var:attacker_state_vs_@ROOT = {
						clr_state_flag = border_incident_active
					}
					var:defender_state_vs_@ROOT = {
						clr_state_flag = border_incident_active
					}
					clear_variable = attacker_state_vs_@ROOT
					clear_variable = defender_state_vs_@ROOT
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
